contextRef=\"CY_PERIOD\"><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA; style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;background:white;mso-highlight:white\">The\n directors are responsible for preparing the report and the financial\n statements in<a></a> accordance with applicable law and\n regulations.</span><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;\"></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA; justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA; text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA; justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA; text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA; background:white;mso-highlight:white\">Company law requires the directors to\n prepare financial statements for each financial year.<a></a> Under\n that law the directors have elected to prepare the financial statements in\n accordance<a></a> with United Kingdom Generally Accepted\n Accounting Practice (United Kingdom Accounting<a></a> Standards\n and applicable law). Under company law the directors must not approve the\n financial statements unless they are satisfied that they give a true and fair\n view of the state of affairs of the company and of the profit or loss of the\n company for that period.<a></a> In preparing these financial\n statements, the directors are required to:</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA; justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA; text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA; background:white;mso-highlight:white\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA; justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:11.6pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA; none;text-autospace:none\"><b><span style=\"font-size:10.0pt;&#xD;&#xA; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;background:white;mso-highlight:white\">·</span></b><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA; background:white;mso-highlight:white\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">   </span>select\n suitable accounting policies and then apply them consistently;</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA; justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA; text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA; background:white;mso-highlight:white\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA; justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:11.6pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA; none;text-autospace:none\"><b><span style=\"font-size:10.0pt;&#xD;&#xA; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;background:white;mso-highlight:white\">·</span></b><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA; background:white;mso-highlight:white\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">   </span>make\n judgements and accounting estimates that are reasonable and prudent; and</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA; justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA; text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA; background:white;mso-highlight:white\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA; margin-left:11.6pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-11.6pt;&#xD;&#xA; line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:11.6pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA; none;text-autospace:none\"><b><span style=\"font-size:10.0pt;&#xD;&#xA; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;background:white;mso-highlight:white\">·</span></b><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA; background:white;mso-highlight:white\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">   </span>prepare\n the financial statements on the going concern basis unless it is inappropriate\n to<a></a> presume that the company will continue in business.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA; justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA; text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:&#xD;&#xA; 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;background:white;mso-highlight:white\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA; justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA; text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA; background:white;mso-highlight:white\">The directors are responsible for keeping\n adequate accounting records that are sufficient to<a></a> show and\n explain the company's transactions and disclose with reasonable accuracy at\n any time the financial position of the company and enable them to ensure that\n the financial statements comply with the Companies Act 2006. They are also\n responsible for safeguarding the assets of the company and hence for taking\n reasonable steps for the prevention and detection of fraud and other\n irregularities.</span><span
